Summary of Important News

Xiang, Yuanling, Hengshan, Xiangtan, Sangzhi, Dong'an, Chenxi, Hengyang, Xinhua, Shimen, Cili, Qiancheng, Guiyang, Yongshui, Xupu, etc., each receive 1,000 yuan; Anhua, Changning, Qiyang, Leiyang, Yongming, Dayong, Anren, Chaling, Youxian, Jiahe, Xintian, Yongxing, Baojing, Huangxian, Chenxian, Yizhang, Lanshan, Xinning, Jingxian, Qianyang, Pingjiang, Liuyang, Yongshun, Longshan, Zhijiang, Shaoyang, Chengbu, Tongdao, Linli, Liling, Ningxiang, Guidong, Guzhang, Zixing, Lingxian, Ningyuan, etc., each receive 500 yuan; Changsha, Taoyuan, and Luxi, etc., each receive 2,000 yuan. In total, 55 counties receive 40,000 yuan. As for the disaster situation in Hunan Province, Representative Pan Zhongqing sent a detailed letter to the Hunan Fellow-Provincials Association in Beijing yesterday, excerpts of which are as follows, to give a glimpse of the situation: "The total area of flooded fields in the province is approximately six million mu. Assuming an average yield of four shi of grain per mu, the total loss is 24 million shi of grain. Valued at five yuan per shi, this amounts to 120 million yuan. Including other losses, the total is estimated at 170-180 million yuan. There are approximately 11 million disaster victims, most of whom are destitute and cannot be settled. Providing relief to these victims is an extremely difficult task. Without active preparation in advance, it will be difficult to manage effectively. From autumn to spring, it is almost a year, and the disaster victims have no grain left. How easy is it to provide them with such a long-term supply of food? Even if the water has receded in the disaster areas in higher ground, it may still be possible to cultivate in the autumn to make up for some losses. However, such disaster areas are few in number. The majority, such as the dozen or so lakeside counties and the areas downstream of the Xiang River, are still submerged in vast floods, and autumn cultivation is impossible, leaving no hope for recovery. In addition, clothing and other necessities have mostly been lost. In the blink of an eye, the weather will turn cold, and in addition to food, funds must be raised for warmth, which is also a huge amount. Moreover, epidemics are likely to occur after the disaster, and medical treatment cannot be delayed. If no work is done to repair the breached dikes after the water recedes, next year's cultivation will also be hopeless. Advance planning cannot be achieved with a small amount of money. Therefore, the things that should be seriously and urgently attended to today are food, clothing, medicine, and dike repair. There are a thousand and one things to do, and it is difficult to describe the situation in words. The relief authorities now regard the disaster situation in Hankou and other places as serious, but they may be neglecting the disaster in Hunan. It is difficult to explain this misunderstanding without seeing the actual disaster situation. I beg you to tell the relief authorities as much as possible." (September 9)

Record of the Opening of Three Congee Kitchens in Wuchang 57

▲ More Than 24,000 Disaster Victims Received Food on the First Day

The Provincial Office of the Hubei Flood Emergency Relief Association set up three congee kitchens, all of which were completed on the 9th. They officially opened today (the 10th) at 8:00 AM. That day, Mr. Xiang Yangzhi of the office, Liang Shichun, representative of the National Youth Association, and Di Ernai (an American), Zhang Yaobin, directors of the Wuchang YMCA, and Tang Yasheng, Yi Lansheng, Sun Echi, directors of the office, set out to investigate in order to improve and benefit the disaster victims. The conditions of each congee kitchen are recorded separately as follows: (1) First congee kitchen: Located at Meijiashan outside Tongxiang Gate, the person in charge is Xu Chengfa. The assisting directors are from the Sanshan, Peishan, Zhishan, and Chengshan halls. Local gentry started the fire to cook congee from 12:00 PM on the 9th, and the kitchen opened at 8:00 AM on the 10th, closing at 2:00 PM. According to Director Xiang, the kitchen will need to extend its hours by one or two hours in the future to allow disaster victims to enter and eat at their leisure. He also ordered a detailed report of the daily needs for rice, firewood, charcoal, and water for budgeting purposes. (2) Second congee kitchen: Located at Changchun Temple outside Binyang Gate. Upon investigation, more than a thousand disaster victims were seen sitting on the ground waiting for food. As the scheduled time had passed, the kitchen was rushing to cook more congee. The person in charge is Hou Shuide (a Taoist priest), the abbot of Changchun Temple. He has considerable experience in distributing congee, so the order and arrangement were even better than the first kitchen. It is said that a total of 23 dan of rice were cooked, and approximately 9,600-700 disaster victims received food. The kitchen closed at 4:00 PM. (3) Third congee kitchen: Located at Baotong Temple on Hongshan. The location is spacious, the layout is perfect, and the order is excellent. The abbot of the temple, Wenxian (a monk), is also very enthusiastic and has sent 52 monks to assist in the cooking and distribution of congee. When the kitchen opened at 8:00 AM, there was an endless stream of people. A total of 14 dan of rice were cooked, and 5,000-6,000 disaster victims received food. It is said that the mat sheds nearby have not yet been fully completed, and the number of disaster victims will inevitably increase daily. In total, the three kitchens cooked 55 dan of rice, and approximately 24,000 disaster victims received food.

Shandong to Launch Large-Scale "Purification of the Countryside" 58

Jinan Dispatch: Regarding the issue of purifying the countryside in Shandong and Henan, Han Fuju has already gone to Bian to negotiate with Liu Zhi and has reached a compromise. After Han returned to Jinan, he convened a meeting of Shandong generals to discuss suppressing bandits in order to launch a large-scale purification of the countryside throughout the province. Important generals currently in Jinan include Ma Hongkui, Commander of the 15th Route; Zhan Shutang, Commander of the 81st Division; Qiao Lizhi, Commander of the 74th Division; Ma Guanyi, Commander of the 221st Brigade; Li Yizhi, Commander of the 220th Brigade; Cao Fulin, Commander of the 29th Division; Li Hanzhang, Commander of the 85th Brigade; and Sun Tongxuan, Commander of the 22nd Division, who is in Zhoucun but is expected to arrive in Jinan today, so the meeting can be held tonight. According to Zhang Yue, Counselor of the Countryside Purification Supervision Office, the methods for purifying the countryside in Shandong and Henan provinces will be implemented in accordance with the previously announced detailed rules for purifying the countryside. Ordinary county purification will be carried out on a county basis. In areas with bandits, or where several counties are designated as special zones, purification will be carried out. In Henan Province, large groups of bandits will be eliminated by the military headquarters, while small groups of bandits will be dealt with by the purifying counties. Shandong has decided to start first. Tang Yaoxun's 65th Brigade has already taken two trains south to Tengxian today to suppress bandits in Mengshan (September 11).

Shanxi Rehabilitation Association Urges Yan to Leave Shanxi 59

Urges Yan to Consider the Peace and Tranquility of Shanxi

Taiyuan Dispatch: It has been more than a month since Yan Xishan returned to Shanxi from Dalian. Letters and telegrams from all sides urging him to leave Shanxi are pouring in like snowflakes, but Yan has not been moved in the slightest. When Yan first returned to Shanxi, various parties here paid close attention, but recently, as Yan has been living in seclusion in his hometown without any news, they have become indifferent. However, the Shanxi Rehabilitation and Advancement Association still hopes that Yan will leave Shanxi as soon as possible, so yesterday they sent a letter urging him. The original letter is as follows: "Mr. Bochuan, Greetings. It is said that a defeated general is not worthy of discussing courage, and the husband of a vanquished nation cannot coexist with the nation. Therefore,侥倖 seeking credit is bound to be wrong, and retreating in the face of difficulty is better. You were reckless in waging war last year, and fled after defeat. Although it is said that the situation was dire and you had no choice, the fact is that once you left, the planes stopped coming and the pursuing troops stopped advancing. Your departure at that time saved many. It is a pity that when you left, you did not say a word to apologize to the world, nor did you say a word to comfort the people of Shanxi. Instead, you withdrew a huge amount of cash from the provincial treasury, causing the provincial currency to plummet and leaving everyone unable to make a living. You ruled Shanxi with the people of Shanxi for twenty years. How did the people of Shanxi let you down that you should be so unkind? One who has great ambitions for the world would not do such a thing. Moreover, although you left, the troops are stationed throughout our province, and the bandits are growing stronger by the day. The people are burdened by requisitions and threatened by looting, dying either from starvation or slaughter. Who is to blame for this calamity? It is hardly necessary to elaborate. This is just a brief account of man-made disasters. As for the natural disasters caused by misfortune, the prolonged and severe drought is unprecedented in recent decades. Alas, the people of Shanxi are suffering in this era, with many ways to die and no way to live. If they were not inherently gentle, they would have already rebelled, and the slightest provocation would have aroused a hundred responses, causing unrest. Is the current state of affairs not a miracle? Now, fortunately, after enduring pain for a long time, Heaven and man have shown compassion, and signs of life are beginning to emerge. But you suddenly flew back on an aircraft, announcing that you were waiting for your father's illness. Of the more than 17 million people in Shanxi, do you alone have parents? Last year's tragedy, from a national perspective, left countless people as fatherless, sonless, or wifeless. Xiang Yu lost eight thousand Jiangdong soldiers and said he had no face to see the elders of Jiangdong. How do you compare to Xiang Yu, having lost all the sons and daughters of Shanxi? Yet you insist on seeing your father? Although, we do not mean that children should not care for their parents, nor do we object to you reuniting with your father. You informed the General and Deputy Commander when you first returned, so the general public believes that the Central Government and you have resolved their differences and made peace. We believe that the national situation is so precarious that it is not appropriate to fight among ourselves. Like many, we do not wish to blame you personally. After much investigation, the facts are not so. According to reports, if you do not voluntarily leave Shanxi, Deputy Commander Zhang will persuade the Shanxi generals to advise you together. We believe that the Shanxi generals are all former subordinates who have recently returned to the Central Government. If this happens, they will be disobeying orders if they refuse, and will be hurting personal feelings if they comply. Leaving aside personal feelings, disobeying orders will likely result in punishment. In order to reduce the burden on the people, the fewer the troops, the better. But today's Shanxi is not the Shanxi of the past. Bandits are everywhere, and the four brigades of the past will be difficult to eliminate. If troops from outside Shanxi are deployed, Shanxi's mountains and ranges are difficult to navigate without knowing their intricacies. Thus, if you seek personal peace, the people of Shanxi may not be able to find peace. Is this not contrary to your original intention when you left last year? Moreover, the financial public debt has been suspended, and the Shanxi currency has plummeted to unprecedented levels in recent months. The Shanxi currency was created by you, so how can you bear to see it ruined by you? Other military and political affairs are also hindered and cannot be resolved, without us needing to spell it out in detail. Therefore, we advise you to think carefully, not to fight against fate, to exercise self-restraint, and to retreat far away, so as not to cause a great disaster for the 17 million people of Shanxi for your own peace. If so, the people of Shanxi will be fortunate, fortunate." (September 9)

Discovery of Nestorian Relics in Fangshan 60

Beijing Dispatch: Professor Saeki Yoshiro of Meiji University in Japan, along with Japanese national Matsumura Yuzo and German Doctor of Law Matsubayashi, went to a site only 100 li southwest of Beijing (about 18 li from Fangxian city in the mountains) on September 6 to investigate Nestorian relics. In the courtyard of the Great Buddha Hall of the Cross Temple, they discovered the "Chongsheng Temple Stele on Three Pots Mountain" and the "Imperial Decree on the Stele of the Cross," both made of marble. Beside the stele, there are two ginkgo trees with a circumference of more than two zhang. Based on the age of these two trees, it is not difficult to know that this is an ancient temple dating back more than a thousand years. The temple was founded in the Eastern Jin Dynasty. It seems that Nestorian monks resided here during the Tang Dynasty. The stele is engraved with a cross measuring one chi four or five cun square, and also with Estrangelo Syriac characters, the meaning of which is "Why do you look and hope?", a sentence from Psalm 35 of the Old Testament. Another stele is engraved with a roughly similar cross, but there are no Syriac characters. However, judging from the patterns on both sides, it can still be known that it was built in the same era. It is regrettable that this type of relic is neglected in the remote mountains. Therefore, Dr. 米 intends to find a way to purchase and donate the stele to the Beijing Museum of Antiquities in order to preserve it. The group returned to Beijing on the 8th of this month. According to historical records, Nestorianism was introduced to Chang'an in the ninth year of Emperor Taizong's reign (635 AD) and flourished in China for 150 years. In the second year of Emperor Dezong's reign (781 AD), the "Stele of the Propagation of Nestorianism in China" was erected in Xi'an, Shaanxi. Currently, in addition to Xi'an and Fangshan County, there is another stone stele with a cross engraved on it in a mountain about seven days' journey from Zhangjiakou.

Tiantu Road Washed Away by Floods 61

Many Bridges Were Destroyed

The Entire Road Is Impassable

Harbin Dispatch: There has been a lot of rain in northern Manchuria recently, and the water level of the rivers has suddenly increased by more than ten feet, overflowing their banks. Although the disaster is not as great as in Jiangnan, the damage to the fields is countless. Jidong has many mountains, and the mountain floods are rushing down with great force, so the disaster is also more serious than in other places. Near the Muleng Ma Bridge on the Hasui Line, the floodwaters are about to submerge the tracks of the East China Railway. The East China Railway Bureau is still sending workers day and night to prevent danger. However, the fields upstream of the Ma Bridge River are most severely flooded. The provincial government has ordered Dongning and Ning'an counties to carry out protective work. However, this has not yet affected transportation. Recently, the mountain floods on the Tiantu route washed away the old Tougou and Xilin River bridges completely on the 1st of this month. The Hailan River bridge was built more solidly, so it was fortunately not broken, but it was submerged by several feet of water. The Badahuazi bridge was also submerged and is in danger. The roadbeds of Shimenzi, Huaiqing, and Jiang'an road platforms have all collapsed for dozens of li due to the turbulent waters. Most of the tracks are submerged in the water. The losses are more than 100,000 yuan. From the 1st to the 4th, there was heavy rain for several days, and railway transportation was completely cut off. The goods accumulated at the stations were also submerged by the water entering the warehouses before they could be moved. It is not yet known when transportation can be restored. Due to the waterlogged railway line, the Longjingcun Wharf was also flooded, and the streets were several feet deep, disrupting traffic. The Longmen and Liu'an bridges on the Hailan River, which connect Longjingcun and Yanji, were hit and destroyed by the wood piled up on the river bank on the evening of the 3rd of this month due to the sudden rise of the river water. Transportation between Longjing and Yanji was also cut off. Fortunately, the water came slowly, and the residents along the river were able to evacuate, so the damage was light. Otherwise, the consequences would have been unimaginable. (September 8)

(33) Record of Conversations between Gannady and Bioni on March 24, 1931 (Describing the Shanghai Labor Unrest and the Communist Party's Activities among Workers)

Regarding the recent week's strike and conflict, Bioni reported as follows:

The Shenxin Textile Factory has already been transferred and is about to shut down. We incited three non-Party workers in the factory to form a Red organization. This organization started a struggle, demanding resumption of operations. A portion of the workers (the factory has four thousand workers) held a meeting and elected seven people to form a committee to carry out the struggle. The committee put forward the following four demands: (1) The textile factory must resume operations. (2) If the factory resumes operations, all wages during the shutdown period should be paid as usual. (3) If the factory changes ownership and reopens, all original workers should retain their positions. (4) If the factory closes down permanently, each worker should be paid five years' wages by the old owner. There is a Yellow Union in the factory, and the workers demanded repayment of the membership fees paid to the union in the last three years. In the past, there was a mutual aid organization, and the workers also demanded repayment of the funds paid to the organization. The leader of our organization has left the factory to take up another job, so now there are only two people left in the organization. Before the factory closed, we sent a comrade to work there (for some reason, this comrade is not in the group of three). He is currently leading this struggle. Yesterday, the committee of seven held a meeting and decided to continue the struggle based on the aforementioned demands. The leaders of the Yellow Union also demanded that the workers oppose the factory's closure, but only based on avoiding unemployment. We are still fighting for the aforementioned demands in order to oppose their propaganda. The Yellow Union had no vitality in the past, only a committee. The (right-wing) within the factory is also very active, accusing our comrades, saying that they have just returned from W place and support the Fourth Plenary Session. There was also a brief strike in the weaving department of the Shenxin No. 1 Textile Factory in the West District (30 workers). They worked twelve hours a day and only received a wage of 34 cents, so they demanded an increase to 42 cents. This demand was agreed to by the supervisor. Then the workers demanded that the daily wage be changed to 52 cents, and the supervisor also agreed. This struggle was led by a committee of eight people, and they were all volunteers. We are carrying out propaganda, demanding that all workers in the factory have their wages increased by 20 percent. We posted eight wall posters on the factory walls. We plan to organize a Red organization there. Sixty workers in the packing department of the Jihe (transliteration) Textile Factory went on strike. These packers originally bundled twenty small packages into one large package, but now they are being forced to increase the number to thirty-two packages. They originally calculated wages by piece, and those with better work ability could earn 80 cents to one yuan per day. Now the factory management is implementing a daily calculation, working twelve hours a day for a wage of 50 cents. After hearing this, four workers went to the management to demand that wages still be calculated by piece, and if calculated by day, the wage must be increased to 55 cents. The management personnel threatened them, saying that if they incited the workers, they would be punished by dismissal. Therefore, all the packers declared that if their demands were not met, they would have to strike. The management finally granted their request and still calculated wages by piece. After this struggle occurred, we formed a Red organization composed of three people and are now trying to pull the aforementioned four workers into it.

The Minxing (transliteration) Silk Weaving Factory has eighty workers. Last year, each person could weave twenty feet of silk per day, earning three cents per foot, or sixty cents per day. The management decided to change the wage to five cash per foot, so the workers went on strike in protest and spontaneously organized a strike committee. We are planning to contact these strikers to organize and guide them.

There are three textile factories in the French Concession, with a total of one thousand workers. One of them is the Dingxin (transliteration) Textile Factory. The Kuomintang has organized a Yellow Union in the factory. Four people who worked hard for the union were dismissed, so the workers sent representatives to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition. The bureau replied that it needed to investigate first before it could handle the matter. The workers were very angry when they heard this, saying that since the four people had already been dismissed, it would be difficult to wait patiently for the results of the investigation. Therefore, they gathered several workers and proposed demanding that the management rehire the dismissed workers. This meeting was held in the house of a woman, and her husband is a Party member. When the Party member heard this, he proposed that the workers in the factory should have an organization and demand that the dismissed workers be reinstated. If this was not allowed, then the only option was to strike. They accepted this proposal and said that they would engage in organization after returning. We don't know what the result will be.

There is a sawmill with a total of two hundred workers, most of whom are short-term workers. They work twelve hours a day and earn 50 to 60 cents. They demanded long-term work and a 20 percent increase in wages. The supervisor only allowed a 20 percent increase in wages but did not allow long-term work.

In the last two weeks, our organizational work in the West District has developed. The Shenxin No. 1 Textile Factory already has a Red organization composed of eight people. Four workers from the Dafeng Textile Factory have contacted us. The Zhentai Textile Factory already has a Red organization composed of three people. One worker from the Fifth Textile Factory, opened by a Japanese company, has contacted us. Four workers from the Honghongsheng have contacted us. Three workers from the Jihe Textile Factory have contacted us. Four workers from the Wenmozhao (transliteration) Factory have contacted us. A flour mill already has a Red organization composed of eight people. One worker from the Puhai (transliteration) No. 2 Textile Factory has contacted us, and one person from a silk reeling factory has also contacted us. In total, there are already thirty-eight workers, and only two of them are Party members. (We asked the other diligent Party members in the West District whether they paid attention to the necessity of all Party members undertaking this important work. Bioni said he would consider this matter.)

Regarding the telephone workers' struggle, we convened a mass meeting last week, with a total of one hundred people attending, but only forty people remained until the end of the meeting. These forty people elected seven people to form a struggle committee to guide this struggle. Our comrades do not know how to utilize this committee. They instead said that a Red trade union should be organized, without discussing the demands that should be put forward or the methods of carrying out the struggle. The workers believe that it is not yet the time to organize a trade union, so we have not yet organized the more active workers into a Red organization, but instead sent several comrades to lead. The workers only asked who they were and showed no signs of trust. Only one of the seven members of the committee is a comrade of our Party. When we reconvened the committee meeting, several members did not attend. Therefore, we told our comrades that the working methods must be changed. We have now organized a Red organization, which has a total of seven people. We are also relying on this organization to carry out work and no longer sending comrades to guide. We are now asking this organization to convene a representative meeting to discuss the demands that should be put forward and the methods of carrying out the struggle. The workers proposed organizing a club instead of organizing a Red trade union. Our Party has expressed its agreement to this. From the above, it can be seen that our comrades still do not know the methods of work. (Then Bioni raised several questions, namely regarding the organization and working methods of maritime workers. We then answered them based on the existing pamphlets.)

(35) An English Report to (Akers) Describing the Struggles of Chinese Textile Workers, Especially the Strikes of Shanghai Silk Reeling Workers

The purpose of this letter is to let you know a little about our work in the textile industry here. The objective situation of the textile industry is very suitable for our work, but because our organization has no contact with textile workers, there are no achievements to speak of in this promising area. Now we can understand that in the past, under the leadership of Li Shan, the lower-level Party departments did not pay attention to the work among the masses, and everything was done by the upper-level (leaders), without considering the work of the trade union at all. Although our Party has now recognized the importance of this work and has sent more capable comrades to lead the work of the trade union, we still have a bad trend that must be improved. We must make the National Labor Union and the Party department realize the separation between the two. We should regard the Party department as an organization for organizing political demonstrations and carrying out political work, and regard the National Labor Union as an organization for carrying out daily economic struggles. Just look at the fact that when the Red trade union wants to carry out certain work during a strike, the Party members in the factory or manufacturing plant where the strike is located mostly do not try to help, and you can see the proof. For example, during the Shanghai silk weaving workers' strike in March and April of this year, the Party department sent nine comrades to work, but even these nine people left their jobs after a few days. Although we have repeatedly explained the necessity of the Party department sending Party members to help the silk weaving workers' strike, only nine comrades were able to use their talents to help such a large struggle of Shanghai workers. We have repeatedly tried to break the separation between the Party department and the National Labor Union and have now achieved some success.

Page 10

The statistics of strikes here are very inaccurate, so we have transferred this work to ourselves in order to seek its increasing accuracy. In the ten weeks since April 30, according to the information we have collected, there have been as many as one hundred and forty-nine strikes. Among them, thirty occurred in textile factories, and thirty-eight occurred in silk weaving factories. In addition, there was also a large strike of three thousand female workers in hair braiding factories in North China. There were also several strikes in cigarette factories and match factories. There was also a strike of apprentices in a textile factory, with a total of seventy strikes by female workers. The number of people in a single strike ranges from several hundred to 20,000. These types of strikes are naturally spontaneous. The total number of strikes is naturally more than our records, because our source of information is newspapers, and newspapers definitely do not publish all strike news.

There are more than one hundred silk factories in Shanghai, with more than 50,000 workers (women and child laborers). From October to March, the silk factories do not operate. In October of last year, the Yellow Union forced the workers to accept a 15 percent reduction in wages due to the low wholesale price of raw silk. In March of this year, the workers began to struggle, demanding the restoration of their original wages. From March 9 to April 3, workers went on strike separately, totaling thirty-one strikes. On April 4, thirty-two silk factories jointly launched a general strike, with a total of 20,000 workers on strike. On April 11, the Social Affairs Bureau prohibited workers from striking, but on April 18, the workers held another general strike, with thirty-three silk factories participating. The Social Affairs Bureau, the City Party Department, and the Yellow Trade Union urged the workers to resume work and guaranteed the restoration of wages. The Social Affairs Bureau decided to increase wages, to be implemented from June 1. However, on June 1, the silk factories suddenly announced a shutdown, notifying the workers to wait for the government to approve the silk industry public bonds before receiving the increased wages. Therefore, the city of Andong in the three eastern provinces became known for the strike of 15,000 workers.

There is no Party department or trade union organization in the silk factories. Before the Shanghai silk factory workers went on strike, it was said that the Communist Youth League had a centralized organization in the Shanghai silk factories, but by the time of the strike, this organization was no longer visible. On March 15, I met female comrades from the Women's Committee of the National Labor Union and discussed with them the methods of dealing with the silk industry situation. We decided to use the relationship established on March 8 and start working among the workers, but this work has not yet been implemented. The National Labor Union, SLC, and the local Party affairs committee are all under pressure to deal with the current situation in the silk industry and have no time to take care of it. Even printing materials or even printing a page of large characters has therefore been transferred to the Party department for handling. These groups have held many meetings, and there have been many good resolutions regarding the work in the silk industry. The Party department and SLC specially sent a comrade to lead the work in the silk industry, but no comrade is responsible for the work among the silk reeling workers. We had a prediction that silk reeling workers would launch a large-scale strike, but several comrades in leading positions in the Shanghai group still disagreed, even though they saw news of silk reeling workers' strikes every day. When the general strike was in progress, we proposed convening a workers' representative congress but were also opposed. Finally, after our repeated persuasion, these comrades realized that their views were wrong and agreed to find a way to convene this meeting and publish a special issue the next day (April 18), advising the workers to change the item of (organizational rights) into a concrete demand and publicly put forward the slogans of (oppose arbitration) (support direct negotiations) and (organize the workers' own committee). However, these conditions were not fulfilled. I believe that this strike of silk reeling workers is enough to make the comrades of the Party department and the National Labor Union realize that although the workers have the determination to fight, the fact that our Party's organization has no contact with this struggle is a great regret. The current working methods are being improved, which can be seen in the records of our conversations with the comrades who share the existing duties. We have not only told the National Labor Union about the lessons learned from the silk reeling workers' strike, but have also drafted an official document and submitted it to the Party department in charge of this duty. Attached is a document to the National Labor Union on the situation of the cotton industry.

Regarding the situation of the textile industry outside of Shanghai, we have obtained very little information. We have repeatedly requested the National Labor Union to establish a large-scale National Textile Industry Provisional Committee.

In addition, several comrades have also deeply believed that these strikes, the frequency of which is increasing and the nature of which is becoming more and more widespread, are definitely not the workers' usual seasonal struggles, but the result of the oppression of the workers' lives. This oppression is related to the current global economic crisis. Japanese imperialists are the largest owners of Chinese textile factories. Now, under the influence of this global economic crisis, they want to compensate for their losses with the workers, and British imperialists also have similar plans. You can see this in the aforementioned document on the cotton yarn industry.

The strikes in textile factories are only the prelude to a large-scale strike in the cotton industry. The large-scale strike in the future will definitely not be just a struggle against Chinese textile factory owners, but also a large-scale struggle against British and Japanese cotton employers. The British Far East Economic Survey Group's suggestion to the British cotton magnates was (to make sacrifices in all classes) to adapt to the market situation and invest more capital in Chinese textile factories. The Manchester Yellow Union has already accepted the group's suggestion and agreed to reduce the wages of Manchester dye industry workers. We have advised the National Labor Union to publish a petition, asking British cotton workers to recognize the stakes. I think that if MM could make the same petition to Chinese cotton workers, it would definitely help the cotton workers' movement in both countries. I don't know what you think. If you also think so, please be sure to send the petition from MM here.

Regarding women's work, we have issued an eleven-page pamphlet, which is sent by our trade union to everyone concerned, as a guide for women's work. There is also a questionnaire attached from various countries, in order to learn about women's lives and the general situation of our work among women. Reports that meet our needs are very difficult to find. Except for a women's conference held by Japan during a certain strike, there are no achievements to speak of in women's work. Even the necessary agencies in the white areas of China have not been established. In China, we did establish a weak agency in the upper-level Party department, but it has been almost completely destroyed due to recent arrests and the incitement work of a certain CC (Communist Party) member. We have discussed how to establish this work in the Party department and the National Labor Union. The main work we focus on is that the women's committee in the Party should guide the work of the trade union among women. The main work at present should be to establish a Red trade union and seek practical results. Therefore, the WD (Women's Department) in the Party should urgently guide and assist the National Textile Committee and help it draft a work plan regarding the re-establishment of the Women's Committee and its current work. We are also conducting this jointly with the National Labor Union. We have sent several women to the Soviet area to work, but have not yet received a report.

Local Correspondence

Jinshan 63

Villager Gu Ada Tragically Tortured to Death with Private Punishment. Gu Shenshi, a widow from Qinxixiang, Zhangyan Sixth District, is approaching fifty years of age. Her husband has been dead for many years, and she only has one son named Ada, who is now twenty-five years old. Last autumn, he married the daughter of Gan Abao from Jinweixiang as his wife. Ada is usually law-abiding and dedicated to agriculture. The other day (the 10th), Ada's uncle-in-law's family had a tangbing feast, and Ada went to the feast because he was a relative. That night, his father-in-law insisted on him staying overnight, so he did not go home. Unexpectedly, in the middle of the night, Captain Tan of the Jinshan Water Patrol Team led more than ten patrol officers and, on the pretext of searching for bandits, arrested Ada without discrimination and escorted him to Langxia. The Water Patrol Team headquarters did not ask about the situation and immediately used extreme torture to force a confession. Ada was indeed a kind-hearted farmer and only cried out for injustice. Later, because he was subjected to extreme torture, he vomited blood from his mouth and his breath was as thin as a thread. Seeing that he had caused trouble, Captain Tan secretly sent patrol officers to carry him by boat to the wild Shantang area west of Kongjiaque and threw Ada into the water to try to cover up the traces. Unexpectedly, he was spotted by the local villagers there, who called for help and rescued Ada. However, he eventually died from his injuries. Afterwards, the corpse's mother, Gu Shenshi, together with the village head, Hu Dajun, reported the incident to the Zhangyan Sixth District Office and the First Public Security Bureau. Later, the district office and the public security bureau both used telephones to report to the county government, requesting that officials be sent to examine the corpse, punish the murderers, and vindicate the deceased. Captain Tan had already gone to the county government to fabricate a false confession and falsely claimed that Gu Ada was trying to escape, fell into the water, and drowned in order to shirk his responsibility. Local people were indignant when they heard this. Mo Jun Menghui, the standing committee member of the Fifth District Branch of the Party Department, has also begun to investigate in order to report the incident.

The county government also has the same resolution and has recorded the case and submitted it to the provincial departments for approval. Gambling Leads to Murder. Songjiang 65

A Word on Urging the Repair of the Seawall. After the Jinshanwei seawall was destroyed by strong winds, heavy rain, and huge waves on the 25th of last month, sections one and two of the Xitang section, another heavy rain on the 6th of this month put section three at risk. The people of Songjiang and Jinshan sent telegrams to appeal and rushed to report the danger, and the situation was very tense. Everyone thought that the August flood season was approaching, and if it was not blocked in advance, it would be difficult to avoid becoming a sequel to Gao Shao. Regarding the repair funds, 10,000 yuan has been borrowed from the county's road construction land donation item and handed over to the Seawall Works Office to receive it. However, because Director Xue has been late in arriving, work has not yet started, and the people are panicked and indescribable. Yesterday, Director Xue and technician Shen Baozhang came to Songjiang to discuss the situation of the seawall repair project with County Magistrate Shen and Construction Bureau Chief Sun. County Magistrate Shen, considering the importance of the matter, immediately invited the leaders of various Party, government, military, and academic institutions and local gentry to hold a discussion meeting. Director Xue reported on the spot that the Jinshanwei seawall project was in a very critical situation, and the estimated cost of the repair was about 35,000 yuan. Now there is a shortage of both people and money, and it is planned to submit a request to the provincial departments for funds. I have to return to Shanghai tomorrow morning due to a matter, he said. Everyone present expressed their dissatisfaction, saying that the exchange of official documents would take time, and the autumn flood season was approaching. Once the angry tide surged, the Songjiang and Jinshan areas would become a swamp, and millions of lives would suffer together. Moreover, whether the provincial departments can allocate funds is still a question. The funds have already been borrowed for 10,000 gold, and Commander Cao has agreed to allocate a team to help. If the funds are insufficient, the local area will also temporarily agree to raise funds, which will be returned by the Construction Department in the future, they said. After a detailed explanation from everyone, Xue finally relented. After discussion, they immediately rushed to prepare disaster relief materials that night, hired ships to transport them, and the issue of workers required about six or seven hundred workers a day. In addition to the two hundred existing workers from the Seawall Works Office and one hundred workers from the Construction Bureau, the conscription system was implemented, and if it was insufficient, a request was made to allocate troops to assist. It was decided that all those present would rush to Jinshanwei this morning to investigate. If the weather is clear during the day, then the great tide until the eighteenth day of the lunar calendar can be safely passed.

Wuxi 66

Water Thieves Rob Night Boats. The Jiangyin Zhouzhuang night boat, which travels between our county and Jiangyin, was suddenly encountered by a pirate ship at 0:30 AM yesterday, when it was passing through the Yangqihe ferry crossing in our county. More than ten bandits jumped out, armed with weapons such as handguns, Mauser pistols, chisels, and sharp knives, shouting to stop the boat. The thieves then boarded the boat one after another and looted wantonly. Forty silver dollars, dozens of silver coins, six cotton quilts, and foreign goods such as toothbrushes, face cloths, and foreign socks carried by the foreign goods store were robbed, worth more than 30 silver dollars. As for the passengers, they were robbed of about two or thirty silver dollars. After the thieves got their loot, they jumped back to their original boat and prepared to speed away. Suddenly, they saw another open boat coming nearby, and they boarded the boat again and robbed arbitrarily. After about half an hour, they were able to leave with their loot. After checking, it was estimated that clothing and other items worth more than one hundred silver dollars had been robbed.

Silk Factories Obtain Public Bonds but Do Not Start Work. The Silk Factory Industry and Trade Union in our county recently stated that the owners of Yongyu Silk Factory outside the South Gate, Zhu Zhuxian, etc., did not start work after obtaining silk industry public bonds, and they did not purchase raw materials, and the factory site was being returned. Measuring their private intentions, it was nothing more than cleverly seizing public funds to relieve people's livelihood in order to satisfy their desire to repay debts and enrich themselves, disregarding the laws of the national government and the lives of workers. There are also Yuanfeng, Xifeng, Yonghengfeng, Yishengyu, Daxin, and other factories that have also obtained public bonds, and their attitude is unusually silent, and to this day there has been no news of preparing to start machinery for business. What their intentions are can be imagined. Therefore, yesterday, they submitted a request to the county government for verification and quick transfer to the Ministry of Industry and the Silk Industry Public Bond Custody Committee for strict sanctions in accordance with laws and regulations to save unemployment and stabilize people's livelihoods. Wang Daoan's Family, the Notorious Thief, Executed by Firing Squad. Wang Daoan's family, a Jiangbei doctor in Dalou Lane, Qingshi Old Righteous Village, in our city, was robbed by thieves at 5:00 AM on July 9. Afterwards, Captain Xue Furui of the Public Security Bureau's detective team led detectives to Shanghai to arrest Zhou Xinshun, the main culprit in the case (i.e., Zhou Xiaoxiazi), and two suspects, coachmen Zhang Xiaosanzi, who were escorted back to the county. After County Magistrate Chen opened the court for interrogation, Zhou Xinshun confessed to robbing Wang Daoan's family. County Magistrate Chen specially approved the death penalty from the provincial government and executed the thief Zhou Xinshun by firing squad at the South School Field at 11:00 AM yesterday. The suspect Zhang Xiaosanzi was interrogated yesterday and was released on bail because there was no major suspicion.

Changzhou 67

Escape of a Local Prisoner: Wu Yi local prison's kitchen duties are assigned by selecting from among the prisoners. On the morning of the 12th, at 6:00 AM, guard Zhou Hanqing escorted convicted thief Chen Mazi to purchase vegetables outside. Due to the crowded marketplace, Chen seized the opportunity to escape. Zhou Hanqing noticed and pursued, but could not find him. Zhou had to return to the prison to report to warden Wu Guoguang. Wu immediately dispatched police to search in all directions, but without success. A request was then submitted to the County Court and County Government for consideration and action.

Soil Merchant Bribes Clerk: Wang Yin, wife of soil merchant Wang Chengji of Wu Yi's Xi Xiasu, was arrested by the County Court Procuratorate. Subsequently, Wang also surrendered himself and was detained. The previous night, Tan Zuoqing, accompanied by Ma Jin'an, went to the residence of Luo Zheng, the chief clerk of the Procuratorate, seeking an audience and offering a hundred yuan banknote as a gift, requesting Luo to arrange for the release of Wang Chengji and his wife. Luo refused, but Tan and Ma left the banknote on the table. The next day, Luo reported this to Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongyi, who immediately ordered the police to arrest Tan and Ma. On the 12th, the court opened an inquiry and found the facts to be true, ordering them to be detained pending prosecution.

Nantong 68

Overflowing Number of Refugees, Difficult to Accommodate: Refugees from various counties north of the Yangtze River are transported to Nantong in batches. Eight reception centers have been set up for men and women, originally intended for two thousand people. However, over three thousand refugees have arrived in recent days, with more than two thousand still on the way. There is no way to accommodate them. On the 12th, the Relief Association requested the County Government to telegraph the Provincial Government for a large sum of relief funds to be allocated to Nantong to subsidize the effort, while urgently dispatching ships to disaster areas to resettle refugees in other counties.

Yao Port Suffers Flooding from Rising Tide: Around midnight on the 11th, the Jiangchao tide surged over ten feet in the Yao Port area of Nantong, breaching the embankment and causing flooding. Fortunately, there was no wind or rain, and the water receded by the morning of the 12th. Efforts are now being made to quickly repair the breaches.

Jiangyin 69

The Saga of Destroying and Re-sculpting City God Statues: After the City God Temple idols were destroyed two years ago, the temple was sealed. Last year, Taoists raised funds and sculpted a gilded City God statue in the main hall, costing over four hundred yuan. Recently, the County Party Department moved into the City God Temple to use as an office. Committee member Xi Hanping, believing the imposing idols were an eyesore, initially wanted to demolish them. However, Section Chief Zhu Tianying ordered craftsmen to build a brick wall around it, temporarily preserving it. Unexpectedly, the Taoists, citing the National Government's regulations protecting temples, tore down the wall the day before yesterday, revealing the gilded City God. Upon seeing this, Committee member Xi became enraged. On the 11th, he notified the Taoists of the Dongyin Shanfang, ordering them to move the statue within a specified period, or it would be demolished to eliminate superstition.

County Executive Supervisory Committee Scheduled to Take Over: The executive supervisory committee members of the County Party Department have been identified by the Provincial Reorganization Committee. After receiving the notification certificates, they held a discussion meeting on the 11th and decided to take over the County Reorganization Committee on the 14th. Jiang Liquan, Zhang Woting, and Sun Guanming were nominated as the receivers.

Yangzhou 70

Small Steamer Company Dedicated to Transporting Disaster Victims: Various small steamer companies operating on inland rivers have agreed to resume service on the 15th, operating the Zhenjiang-Taizhou, Zhenjiang-Yangzhou, and Zhenjiang-Gaoyou routes. Specifically, companies such as Fuyun are showing compassion for disaster victims by offering a public relief steamer for refugees. Those holding passes from various reception centers will be exempt from fares, and passengers will not be allowed on these relief boats. Passenger steamers will also not accommodate refugees to avoid overcrowding.

Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition to Aid Yangzhou: Yangzhou calligraphers and painters, such as Jin Jianwu, have initiated a calligraphy and painting exhibition to raise funds for disaster relief. The exhibition opened on the 12th, selling 1,100 tickets (at two yuan each) and featuring 1,300 works of calligraphy and painting.

Monk of Great King Temple Arrested: Recently, a certain boat delivered a snake-shaped, square-headed object, commonly referred to as the Great King, to the Great King Temple in Yangzhou's Shahepa. Worship flourished. On the 12th, the Public Security Bureau ordered the arrest of the temple's abbot and retrieved the so-called Great King. It is said to have been found dead in a box. Many superstitious men and women are shocked.

Rugao 71

Sea Bandits Land and Harass Juegang: At 5:00 PM on the 7th, seventeen bandit ships carrying two to three hundred sea bandits reportedly equipped with rifles, box cannons, and pistols arrived in the Nankan area of Juegang, Rugao. In the afternoon, they killed a resident on the Beikan beach. That evening, they fired shots as a show of force in Nankan Port, all the way to Niucheqiao, and kidnapped seven people, including residents Liu Wenxu, Wang Xuedao, Bao Wansheng, Ma San's father and son, and two daughters (approximately eighteen or nineteen years old). Upon hearing the news, the Dayu Town Security Corps immediately led a team to pursue them to the coast. Around 6:00 PM on the 8th, the bandits burned two fishing boats moored in the port. The director of the coastal defense corps, upon hearing the alarm, submitted a written report to the County Government on the 9th, requesting urgent assistance. Furthermore, on the 6th, over twenty bandit ships sailed from the north into the waters of the Sixteenth General Office of Changsha Town.

Hangzhou 72

Another Criminal Apprehended in Longjing Kidnapping Case: In the case of the kidnapping and murder of Cantonese merchant Li Jiyun, who was killed and his body dumped in the lake at the Longjing Temple in West Lake, three criminals, Wang Yang, Wang E, and Wu Jingyuan, had previously been arrested and executed. It has now been learned that the fugitive Zhang Fang (also known as Lü Zhenya) committed another robbery in Shanghai, was apprehended, and sentenced to five years. The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau sent a police officer to Shanghai to escort him back to Hangzhou for interrogation by the court. Zhang confessed to the kidnapping of Li Jiyun and stated that he received five hundred yuan after the incident. He was ordered to be detained in the detention center pending sentencing.

Foreman Commits Murder, Stabs One to Death: Ling Xufa, the head machine worker at the Hua Feng Paper Mill in Xiaohua, Daguan, Hangzhou, had a dispute with his deputy, Shen Zhikang, over work-related matters. The dispute had been resolved by fellow workers. However, Shen still harbored resentment. As Ling returned to the factory at 8:00 PM, Shen followed him to the factory gate, pulled out a small dagger, and stabbed Ling in the throat. Ling died within five minutes. Prosecutor Chen was dispatched to the scene by the court. The murderer had already been apprehended by the factory guards and handed over to the court for prosecution.

(2) Jinan Defeats Qinghua 80

12-1

Qiu Dongyan Shows His Skills

This group followed the same pattern: the weak could not overcome the strong. In the first half, Jinan was not particularly impressive, winning by only two goals, 2-0. Jinan then launched an all-out attack. Initially, they were repeatedly unable to score, but in the second half, Qinghua could no longer resist and Jinan scored five consecutive goals, making it 7-0. Then, Qinghua's Fu Guangbin desperately broke through Jinan's defense, making it 7-1, avoiding a complete shutout. The game ended with a score of 12-1. Jinan's famous player, Qiu Dongyan, showed off his skills, agile and powerful. Once he reached the goal, he dashed in all directions, facing no resistance. The goal scorers for Jinan were: (1) Qiu Dongyan, 7 goals; (2) Yang Miao, 3 goals; (3) Mei Hongbao, 1 goal.

General Comments on Yesterday's Men's and Women's Track and Field Finals (Liao)

Men's Finals 96

100 Meters

Amidst the spirited sounds of military music, the announcer, with the force of a general issuing commands, proclaimed the start of the men's 100-meter final. The eight men who had qualified were already waiting at the starting line. As they drew lots to determine their positions, those who drew the fifth and sixth lanes grumbled under their breath, for within ten meters of the starting point, these lanes were uneven and unusually soft. Gu Zaiping and Hao Chunde, upon seeing their numbers, simultaneously exclaimed ("Oh dear, unlucky!"). Once the positions were set, the starting gun fired. Gu Zaiping, eager to win, jumped the gun. A second shot was fired, and Hao Chunde was also found to have moved before the signal. Jiang Xiangqing, enforcing the rules rigorously, announced that both Gu and Hao had each committed a foul. A second foul would result in disqualification. At this point, the air was thick with tension, and each runner's breath came in short gasps. During the third start, everyone was cautious and careful, so the start was relatively even, except for Zhong Lianji, who lagged slightly behind. Up to the 50-meter mark, Zhong was still in the rear. At this point, Hao Chunde was in the lead, followed by Yang Kaizuo, then Gu Zaiping, Zhong Lianji, and Lin Guangxing, all very close. After 70 meters, Zhong emerged to the right of Hao, and by the finish line, he had passed everyone to take first place. Hao Chunde, Yang Kaizuo, and Gu Zaiping followed, in that order. Lin Guangxing, still weak from illness, was unable to compete with the other athletes and failed to place. The time was 11.8 seconds, a remarkable achievement considering the strong southerly wind blowing head-on. The reporter is confident that in the upcoming National Games, Zhong will compete with athletes from various provinces and cities to win the championship and bring glory to our city.

200 Meters 97

After Lin Guangxing and Zeng Rongzhong withdrew from the semi-finals, the competition for the 200-meter race was reduced. The final order of finish was identical to the 100-meter race. Yang Kaizuo had made progress, surpassing the veteran Gu Zaiping twice. It was said that Gu Zaiping had lacked practice during the summer vacation, so his performance had declined. The reporter recalls that Gu did not perform well in last year's city games. Superstitiously speaking, Gu seems to have no luck at city games, otherwise, in the Jiangnan University Games and in matches against the McLing and Bai Hong teams, Gu could often finish in the lead, and would not necessarily be defeated by Zhong and Hao.

400 Meters 98

Before the games, everyone believed that the 400-meter championship would belong to Zeng Rongzhong of Jinan University. However, after seeing Guan Changfa's stride and time in the preliminary 400-meter race, which was only one-fifth of a second behind Zeng Rongzhong's, people realized that Zeng had a strong rival. Furthermore, after Zeng Rongzhong withdrew from the 200-meter semi-finals due to physical discomfort, dizziness, and blurred vision, informed observers thought that the 400-meter title was in danger for Zeng, and that Guan Changfa had a great opportunity. The 400-meter race involves both speed and endurance, and it is extremely difficult to win such a fierce competition if one is not feeling well. The results of yesterday's race were as expected: Guan won with a time of 53 and 3/5 seconds. Zeng, after a fierce battle, managed to secure second place, but after finishing, his face was pale, and he lay on the ground for a long time. After some massage, he gradually managed to stand up. When asked about the reason, it was learned that Zeng had been suffering from poor digestion and abdominal discomfort for several days. According to the sports instructor at Jinan University, Zeng usually doesn't pay much attention to his diet and often buys snacks, which has caused him stomach problems. This is the harm of an unrestrained diet. Zeng had previously traveled north with the Jiangnan track and field team and suffered from diarrhea due to improper food, which prevented him from participating in the competition. This newspaper reported on this matter in detail. It is hoped that Zeng will pay attention to food hygiene in the future and avoid eating randomly, because if an athlete's body is not feeling well during training, not only will they be unable to improve, but they will also be unable to maintain their current condition, and may even regress. It is hoped that Zeng will take this to heart.

800 Meters 99

There were twelve runners in the 800-meter final. Zhou Bin led during the first lap, with a lead of about five meters. Until the turn of the second lap, Qiu Lingru caught up from behind. As they entered the grandstand, Qiu was in first place, Chen Xingpei was second, Zhou Bin was third, and Xia Xianwu was fourth. The spectators all thought that the order of finish was set, but Xia Xianwu had excellent stamina and surged forward, passing Zhou Bin and catching up with Chen Xingpei. He finished not far behind Qiu. It was observed that Qiu Lingru consistently ran on the outside lane and tried to take the lead on the turns, which put him at a disadvantage. If Qiu can pay attention to this, his performance should improve.

1500 Meters 100

Zhang Hugen, a native of Korea, had a strong and well-proportioned body, making him an ideal athlete for track and field events. He participated in yesterday's 1500-meter final and led from start to finish. Zhu Shaohua followed closely behind, less than a few meters behind. After three laps, the positions of the leading runners did not change much. After the turn on the third lap, Zhu Shaohua briefly ran shoulder-to-shoulder with Zhang. However, Zhang also exerted himself and realized that this was a critical moment, so he did not relax for a moment. At this point, both runners had great speed, leaving those behind far behind. In the end, Zhang finished first, Zhu finished second, Tang Xianzhou finished third, and Chen Xingpei finished fourth. Someone familiar with the inner workings of Tongji University said that Tang Xianzhou and Zhang Hugen are both students at Tongji. Zhang practices long-distance running every day, usually alone. Seeing that Tang had potential, he often encouraged him and provided guidance. As a result, Tang's performance improved significantly. In that case, Tang is Zhang's disciple, and it is no surprise that both finished in the lead today, making them two outstanding individuals from the same school. Observing Tang's posture and attitude yesterday, he appeared natural and relaxed, showing great potential. It is hoped that Tang will surpass Zhang in the future, which is what the reporter hopes for.

Men's High Hurdles 101

High hurdle talent is extremely difficult to cultivate. In recent years, few new talents have been discovered. Chen Guojun, who emerged at the last National Games, did not participate this time, so the final race lacked excitement. Of the six who qualified for the final, one dropped out before the race, so only five started. Before starting, Cao Yu stretched his legs vigorously on the side of the track. The reporter asked him why he was exerting himself so much. Cao replied, "My leg muscles are injured, and I need to do these exercises to avoid falling over the hurdles." After the start, Cao had great speed and was far ahead of the other four, but he knocked down two hurdles. Spectators were worried about him, but fortunately, he overcame the difficulties. After clearing the first hurdle, they felt relieved. He reached the finish line in just 17.4 seconds, which is not a great time, but it was one of the best performances of the day, considering the headwind and the soft track. The others were far behind.

Men's Medium Hurdles 102

Medium hurdles have only been introduced to this city for about six months, so the event is not very popular. In the five-person final, everyone finished in their positions safely, except for Da Mao (Sun Huipei), who fell and injured himself at the second hurdle before the finish line. Tao Yingjie finished first, Chen Buzhang finished second, Yang Bingyuan finished third, and Zhang Jinrong finished fourth. The times were not good and were far from Tao's national record set at the National Games. Tao ran with his body upright and his head up, indicating a lack of strong abdominal muscles. It is hoped that Tao will practice abdominal exercises more in the future, as well as the 800-meter run, in order to compete with Chen Ling of Beijing at the National Games.

Men's Field Events 103

Shot Put

Fourteen people signed up for the competition, but only half showed up, which is a joke. Among the seven participants, only four threw over nine meters, which was very disappointing. Chen Baoqiu was indeed weakened by illness, throwing only 10.09 meters, finishing third. Cao Yu finished first, with a score of 10.54 meters, which was 1.1 meters less than Chen's score at the National Games.

Triple Jump 104

In recent years, Wang Jihuai has dominated the triple jump in all major and minor sporting events. However, yesterday Wang injured his ankle on the first jump. Although he tried to continue jumping, he was unable to achieve a good score and was eliminated. Wang said that if his ankle swells due to the sprain, he would not be able to participate in the pentathlon or decathlon tomorrow. If this happens, today's all-around competition will be less exciting. Li Lin, who practiced diligently during the summer vacation, made a lot of progress. Yesterday, he jumped 13.04 meters to win first place, which was not easy. Second place went to Liang Tiancheng, third place went to Liu Mengling, and fourth place went to Fan Jiaju, all with scores above 12.3 meters.

Pole Vault 105

The number of participants in the pole vault was the lowest, indicating the difficulty of this event. Yesterday's competition for the championship was expected to be between Cao Yu and Li Lin. When they reached 3.26 meters, all the other competitors were eliminated, leaving only Cao and Li. Unexpectedly, after jumping over 3.26 meters, Cao's old leg injury suddenly caused him pain, so he stopped competing. As a result, Li won first place without much effort, and with this jump, he tied with Wang Jihuai for first place in individual field events. Some say that Li was blessed with good luck.

Javelin Throw 106

The javelin throw is Wang Jihuai's specialty, but yesterday Wang failed, which was considered strange. It was later learned that, as predicted in this newspaper's previous report, Wang lacked practice due to his foot injury, which weakened his arm muscles. Despite his efforts, he only threw over 43 meters, losing to Liu Jiayu, who threw 44.07 meters, and finishing second. Wang also had to prepare for the triple jump, so he quickly threw a few times, which was also a minor cause of his failure. However, in the reporter's view, this situation is a good sign. The veteran's failure shows that there are rising stars.

Women's Track and Field: 50 Meters and 100 Meters 107

Ms. Zhang Ping could have been carefree in the 50-meter and 100-meter races, but since the arrival of Ms. Situ Wei, a famous athlete from Guangdong, she was filled with anxiety. On the one hand, she trained hard day and night, and on the other hand, she inquired about Situ's true strength. Only after the preliminary and semi-final races the other day did she finally feel relieved. However, as a result of this, her performance has improved slightly, which is truly the effect of mutual encouragement. In the competition, Situ finished second in both events.

200 Meters 108

The women's 200-meter race has always been Liu Jingzhen's specialty, but since Ms. Qian Xingsu emerged, Ms. Liu could only retreat. There were seven runners in yesterday's women's 200-meter race. Unexpectedly, at the 100-meter mark, Ms. Li Jingwen suddenly fell, looking very pitiful. As a result, only six reached the finish line. Ms. Li was in a very forward position at the 100-meter mark. If she had not fallen, she might have had a chance of placing. Ms. Li was extremely unlucky.

Low Hurdles 109

Yang Ren is a pillar of the Liangjiang basketball team and is capable in all kinds of sports. She happened to participate in the low hurdles race yesterday and the day before, and unexpectedly won first place. The reporter met the track and field coach of Liangjiang yesterday, who said that Ms. Yang had never practiced low hurdles. Ms. Yang is truly a sports genius. However, if Ms. Qian Xingsu had not fallen in the preliminary race the other day, there would have been a competition between her and Ms. Yang in yesterday's women's low hurdles final.

Page 12

Javelin 110

The women's javelin is a newly created sport in Shanghai. Recalling the spring middle school games, there were very few women participating in the javelin, and among these few, their posture was incorrect. Although there was no surprising progress in yesterday's competition results, the posture, the way of holding the javelin and the turning movements were all satisfactory. This shows the effect of several months of instruction.

Shot Put Final 111

Shot put is originally a competition of body weight. Now that it is applied to women, the effect should be the same. But today's women mostly have slender figures, how can they win this heavy skill competition and get good results. In yesterday's competition, Ms. Han Wanzhen won the first place with a score of 8.11 meters. Her posture was still good.

Notice to National Arts Athletes 112

Tomorrow at 1:00 PM

The Shanghai Municipal Sports Association's Martial Arts Combat Competition is scheduled for the 15th at 1:00 PM. All athletes who have registered to participate in the competition must report before 12:00 PM on that day, so as to arrange the venue. There is a Martial Arts Hall reception at the entrance of the venue. Athletes who have not received the Martial Arts Athlete Certificate and sportswear can collect them from the reception at that time. The martial arts competition will be divided into five weight classes according to the athlete's weight: (1) 182 pounds or more, (2) 165 pounds or more to 182 pounds, (3) 148 pounds or more to 165 pounds, (4) 132 pounds or more to 148 pounds (5) 132 pounds or less. There are three kinds of championships for men and women: 1. Combat, 2. Wrestling, 3. Fencing. There is one championship for each kind and each level.

At about 4 pm, there was a light rain, and the audience stood on their toes, their interest was very high, and it did not diminish due to the rain. Only the track and field finished all finals at about 5 pm, and the visitors left one after another. The baseball game closed later. Scattered short news, summarized as follows,

Zhejiang Provincial Games 124

The track and field ball games were stopped due to rain yesterday

Gold Market Erratic Last Week 128

Entirely Subject to Speculation

▲Swap spread speculators once pushed the price higher. Gold prices fluctuated dramatically last week, influenced by fleeting winds and rain. Daily fluctuations ranged from six, seven, to over ten taels. People were confused and found it difficult to predict the market, due to conflicting international news, particularly the influence of speculation. Starting from over 770 taels at the beginning of the week, the price reached a high of 75 taels and 2 mace on Wednesday, before suddenly plummeting to a low of 54 taels the following day, then hovering around 60 taels. Finally, it dropped another 7 taels and 1 mace, resulting in a total difference of 21 taels and 2 mace during the week. The silver market trended upward, and drafts also lengthened by one and a half notches, likely because the internal bank exchange rate for British gold had exceeded one shilling and three pence. Gold dealers continued to sell, shorting about 1 million pounds of British gold to date, with some hedging transactions. The initial premium was about 30 taels, peaking at over 40 taels, then returning to around 30 taels. Cash reserves were not very abundant, but a certain bank was buying, causing the current swap spread to tend toward an advance, pressuring short positions, hence the temporary rise in gold prices. Currently, the long position parties include Yongheng, Xinheng, a Mr. Luo, Bingxing drafts hedgers, and Mr. Lu. Guangbang Hengxing, Yifeng, etc., have also flipped to long positions. It is also rumored that speculator Mr. Wu, who originally held a short position, has been continuously covering. However, Dalianbang still holds 4,000 to 5,000 short positions, and Yuan Maoyong and Japanese merchants are also short. Merchandise hedgers such as Dadecheng have made some deliveries recently. Will there be a reversal in market prices during the swap spread period? Here is a summary of the week's events: ▲Fleeting winds and rain, daily fluctuations of over ten taels. From Monday (September 7th), the major bill rate rose by 0.0625 to 0.125. The silver price rose by 0.125, the shilling lengthened by half a notch, and the internal exchange rate seemed looser. Dealers sold off a significant amount, causing the gold price to open slightly lower by 1 tael and 2 mace, at 769 taels. The news of a bank failure in the United States had no major impact. Subsequently, selling pressure caused the price to fall to 65 taels and 1 mace, before rising to 69 taels and 3 mace due to hedging purchases. At noon, it fell again to 66 taels and 5, closing at 7 taels and 5. In the afternoon, those who had sold in the morning rushed to cover, causing the price to rise to 72 taels and 1 mace, closing at 71 taels and 6 mace, a gain of 1 tael and 4 mace from the previous Saturday. Mr. Wu, a speculator, bought in. Guangbang went short and then long. The next day, the major bill rate rose again by 0.0625. The silver price was unchanged, the shilling unchanged, and the internal exchange rate was flat. Dealers sold more than they bought. The gold market opened slightly lower by 1 tael and 1 mace, at 70 taels and 4 mace, then 69 taels and 7 mace. Afterwards, buying pressure surged, reaching 73 taels and 7 mace at noon, closing at 3 taels and 3 mace. In the afternoon, it opened flat, then rose to 75 taels. Large players fought to buy, slightly pulling back to 73 taels, closing at 73 and a half taels, a further increase of 1 tael and 9 mace. The market was relatively stable, fluctuating by no more than 5 taels and 3 mace throughout the day. On Wednesday, the major bill rate contracted by 0.0625. The silver price was slightly lower by 0.125, the shilling unchanged, and the internal exchange rate trended upward. Chinese merchants sold heavily. The gold price opened higher by 1 tael and 2 mace, at 74 taels and 7 mace. US stocks saw a small decline, leading to five... On Wednesday, the major bill rate contracted by 0.0625. The silver price was slightly lower by 0.125, the shilling unchanged, and the internal exchange rate trended upward. Chinese merchants all sold. The gold price opened higher by 1 tael and 2 mace, at 74 taels and 7 mace. US stocks saw a small decline, leading to 5 taels and 2 mace. Later, news broke that a silver price conference had been decided upon and a date for convening had been set. Consequently, long position holders such as Chen, Wu, Long, and Luo sold heavily, causing the market price to collapse precipitously, plummeting by over ten taels. The wave was turbulent. At 3:43 PM, it suddenly fell to 56 and a half taels. Guangbang came in to buy, recovering to 59 taels, closing at 7 taels and 8 mace. In the afternoon, buying pressure seemed stronger, showing signs of reversal. A certain bank also bought in, so the price was 61 taels and 4 mace around 3 PM. However, large Indian remittance reports pushed the price back down to 58 taels and 4 mace, closing at 60 taels and 2 mace, a sharp drop of 13 taels and 3 mace from the previous day, with a total difference of 18 taels and 7 mace throughout the day. The next day, the major bill rate rose by 0.0625 to 0.125, the silver price increased by 0.375, the shilling lengthened by one notch, but the internal exchange rate improved. It was truly a case of contrasting bright and dark prospects. The gold price initially opened at 61 and a half taels, then 63 taels. Due to the news that the silver conference had failed, sentiment improved. Suddenly, Mr. Lu sold, causing the price to plunge to 54 taels. Afterwards, large players rushed to buy, closing at 64 taels at noon. There was a difference of 10 taels in half a day. In the afternoon, Indian remittance reports were small and large players bought in. A certain bank also made purchases, so the price rose to 67 and a half taels, closing at 64 taels and 9 mace, a recovery of 4 taels and 7 mace from the previous day, with a total of 13 and a half taels fluctuating. Large players all bought in. On Friday, the major bill rate contracted by 0.0625, the silver price decreased by 0.125, the shilling remained the same, and the internal exchange rate seemed looser. The gold price opened lower by 1 tael and 1 mace, at 63 taels and 8 mace. Later, Wu and Lu rushed to buy in, already exceeding 70 taels, to 71 taels and 8 mace, closing at 70 taels and 2 mace at noon. In the afternoon, there were rumors that India would adopt silver coinage. The market was greatly shocked by this news, and selling pressure intensified, plunging over 7 taels, suddenly to 63 taels and 2 mace. Guangbang bought in again, rising to 66 taels and 8 mace.

By the close, it was 65 taels and 9 mace, still up 1 tael from the previous day. The front and back markets fluctuated a total of 8 taels and 6 mace. On Saturday, the major bill rate rebounded by 0.125, the silver price increased by 0.125, the shilling did not move, and the internal exchange rate seemed looser. The gold price opened at 58 taels and 5, a decrease of 7 taels and 4 mace, because the major bill was expected to contract on the 11th, but it did not, causing sentiment to weaken. It then rebounded from 9 taels and a half to 6 taels and 8 mace. Afterwards, Guangbang bought in again, gradually rising, but fluctuating. Interbank Lending Tight on Sundays 130

Yesterday was Sunday, a bank holiday. News was quiet. The interbank lending rate in the market fell slightly by half a li, to 7 qian 2 fen 4 li 7 hao 5 si in the morning and 7 qian 2 fen 4 li 5 si in the afternoon. The situation was rather sluggish. Due to the bank holiday, the demand for overnight loans was tight, so the rate fell sharply to 2 qian in both the morning and afternoon, a rise of 5 to 6 fen from the previous day, also the highest price in recent days. The amount of drafts made was 335,000 in the morning and 580,000 in the afternoon. There were no transactions in banknotes in either market. The off-market banknote transactions were only 40,000 in the morning and none in the afternoon. Money shops received over 4.7 million in silver public notes and over 41 million in silver public notes. There were no reports of interbank foreign exchange lending due to the holiday.
